# Setup | BaklavaJS

[Skip to content](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/setup.html#VPContent)

Return to top

Setup [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/setup.html#setup)

===============================================================

View Model [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/setup.html#view-model)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

There is one key component you need when using the visual editor: the _view model_. You can create a new view model by using the [`useBaklava`](https://baklava.tech/api/functions/_baklavajs_renderer_vue.useBaklava.html)
 function. The view model has the following type:

ts

    interface IBaklavaViewModel {
        editor: Editor;
        /** Currently displayed graph */
        displayedGraph: Graph;
        /** True if the currently displayed graph is a subgraph, false if it is the root graph */
        isSubgraph: Readonly<boolean>;
        settings: IViewSettings;
        commandHandler: ICommandHandler;
        history: IHistory;
        clipboard: IClipboard;
        hooks: {
            /** Called whenever a node is rendered */
            renderNode: SequentialHook<{ node: AbstractNode; el: HTMLElement }, null>;
            /** Called whenever an interface is rendered */
            renderInterface: SequentialHook<{ intf: NodeInterface<any>; el: HTMLElement }, null>;
        };
        switchGraph: (newGraph: Graph | GraphTemplate) => void;
    }

The view model is reactive so it can be used in watchers, computed properties, etc.

WARNING

The `useBaklava` function accepts an existing editor instance as parameter. However, because of the way Vue's reactivity system works you'll need to use the viewModel.editor property afterwards instead of your own reference to the editor.

Editor Component [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/setup.html#editor-component)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now you can pass the view model to the editor component:

vue

    <template>
        <!--
            By default, the editor completely fills its parent HTML element.
            If you directly use the editor in the <body> element, make sure to use
            a wrapper <div> with specified width and height properties:
            <div style="width: 90vw; height: 90vh">
                <BaklavaEditor :view-model="baklava" />
            </div>
        -->
        <BaklavaEditor :view-model="baklava" />
    </template>
    
    <script setup lang="ts">
    import { BaklavaEditor, useBaklava } from "@baklavajs/renderer-vue";
    import "@baklavajs/themes/dist/syrup-dark.css";
    
    const baklava = useBaklava();

Settings [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/setup.html#settings)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

Settings can be changed by accessing the `settings` property of the view model right after creating it or reactively at any moment later.

### Properties [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/setup.html#properties)

| name | data type | default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| useStraightConnections | boolean | false |
| enableMinimap | boolean | false |
| toolbar.enabled | boolean | true |
| palette.enabled | boolean | true |
| background.gridSize | number | 100 |
| background.gridDivision | number | 5   |
| background.subGridVisibleThreshold | number | 0.6 |
| sidebar.enabled | boolean | true |
| sidebar.width | number | 5   |
| sidebar.resizable | boolean | true |
| displayValueOnHover | boolean | false |
| nodes.defaultWidth | boolean | 200 |
| nodes.maxWidth | number | 320 |
| nodes.minWidth | boolean | 150 |
| nodes.resizable | boolean | false |
| nodes.reverseY | boolean | false |
| contextMenu.enabled | boolean | true |
| contextMenu.additionalItems | ContextMenuItem\[\] | \[\] |
| panZoom.minScale | number | 0.05 |
| panZoom.maxScale | number | 10  |
| zoomToFit.paddingLeft | number | 300 |
| zoomToFit.paddingRight | number | 50  |
| zoomToFit.paddingTop | number | 110 |
| zoomToFit.paddingBottom | number | 50  |

For example, to enable displaying the value of a node interface on hover:

ts

    const baklava = useBaklava();
    baklava.settings.displayValueOnHover = true;

---

# Node Interfaces | BaklavaJS

[Skip to content](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interfaces.html#VPContent)

Return to top

Node Interfaces [​](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interfaces.html#node-interfaces)

================================================================================

Node interfaces define the inputs and outputs of a node. They can be connected to eachother. If the interface is not connected, it can display a Vue component which allows the user to manually set the value of the interface.

Port [​](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interfaces.html#port)

----------------------------------------------------------

Each node interface can have a so-called _port_. The port is used for connecting an output interface of one node to an input interface of another node.

Ports are displayed by default. However, in certain scenarios it is not useful for an interface to have a port. Examples for such scenarios include:

*   An output interface that is only used for displaying data instead of passing it on to other nodes
*   An input interface that is just used for direct input by the user and doesn't expect any data from other nodes

In such cases, the port can be turned off when creating the node interface:

js

    import { NodeInterface } from "baklavajs";
    new NodeInterface("My Interface", 0).setPort(false);

Display Component [​](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interfaces.html#display-component)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As long as a node interface is not connected via its port, it can display a Vue component. The component allows the user to set the value of the node interface manually.

The components receives these props:

*   `modelValue`: The value of the interface. The type of this prop is dependent on the type of the value
*   `node` (type: [AbstractNode](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.AbstractNode.html)
    ): The node instance in which this interface lives
*   `intf` (type: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
    ): The instance of the node interface

To update the value of the interface, the component can emit the `update:modelValue` event with the new value.

Here is an example component, that display a button that, when clicked, increases the value of the interface by one:

vue

    <!-- MyComponent.vue -->
    
    <template>
        <button @click="count">{{ modelValue }}</button>
    </template>
    
    <script>
    import { defineComponent } from "vue";
    
    export default defineComponent({
        props: {
            modelValue: {
                type: Number,
                required: true,
            },
        },
        emits: ["update:modelValue"],
        setup(props, { emit }) {
            const count = () => {
                emit("update:modelValue", props.modelValue + 1);
            };
            return { count };
        },
    });
    </script>

To use this component, use the `setComponent()` function of the node interface:

js

    import { markRaw } from "vue";
    import { NodeInterface } from "baklavajs";
    import MyComponent from "MyComponent.vue";
    new NodeInterface("My Interface", 0).setComponent(markRaw(MyComponent));

WARNING

Use Vue's `markRaw` function, since the node interface will be made reactive. This can cause performance issues (and will also print warnings to the console).

TIP

If you'll be using the node interface multiple times, it makes sense to [create a custom node interface class](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interfaces.html#extending-the-node-interface-class)
.

Middleware [​](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interfaces.html#middleware)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

The node interface class also provides the option to use _middleware_. This can be used to set additional meta-data of the node interface in a type-safe way. A middleware is essentially just a function that is called with the node interface as the first parameter and an arbitrary amount of other parameters.

Let's take the `setType` middleware of the [Interface Types Plugin](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interface-types.html)
 as an example:

js

    function setType(intf, type) {
        intf.type = type.name;
    }
    
    // usage - just an example, the interface types plugin works a bit different
    new NodeInterface("My Interface", 0).use(setType, "number");

As can be seen, the function just sets a new `type` property on the interface to the value it receives as parameter.

Extending the Node Interface Class [​](https://baklava.tech/nodes/interfaces.html#extending-the-node-interface-class)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Always setting the component and middleware when creating a node interface is very tedious and leads to a lot of code duplication. Instead, a new class can be created that extends the base `NodeInterface` (or one of the [pre-defined interfaces](https://baklava.tech/nodes/pre-defined-interfaces.html)
, which in turn are also just subclasses of the base `NodeInterface` class):

js

    import { markRaw } from "vue";
    import { NodeInterface, setType } from "baklavajs";
    import MyComponent from "MyComponent.vue";
    
    class MyNodeInterface extends NodeInterface {
        constructor(name: string) {
            super(name, 0);
            this.setComponent(markRaw(MyComponent));
            // this is just an example, the interface types plugin works a bit different
            this.use(setType, "number");
        }
    }
    
    const i = new MyNodeInterface("My Interface");
    i.value; // -> 0
    i.component === MyComponent; // -> true
    i.type; // -> "number"

---

# Customization | BaklavaJS

[Skip to content](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/customization.html#VPContent)

Return to top

Customization [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/customization.html#customization)

=======================================================================================

Baklava offers many levels of customization, from simple theming up to full-blown custom components.

Theming [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/customization.html#theming)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use a theme by installing the `@baklavajs/themes` package and importing the theme-specific CSS file.

For example:

js

    import "@baklavajs/themes/syrup-dark.css";

There are currently two themes available:

*   Classic (Baklava v1 theme): `classic.css`
*   Syrup Dark: `syrup-dark.css`

Baklava's themes make heavy use of CSS variables. This means that you can easily change colors or other visual properties by overriding the values of the variables in your CSS. Check out [this file](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/themes/src/classic/variables.scss)
 for a list of variables.

CSS Classes [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/customization.html#css-classes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Baklava applies different CSS classes to the HTML elements to make customization via CSS as easy as possible. You can override styles to customize most aspects of the look and feel. Apart from the [standard CSS classes](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/customization.html#list-of-css-classes)
, Baklava also sets certain `data-` properties you can use for styling.

For example, to make all nodes of type `MyNodeType` have a blue background, you can use the following CSS:

css

    .baklava-node[data-node-type="MyNodeType"] {
        background-color: lightblue;
    }

Custom Components [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/customization.html#custom-components)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If these options don't fulfill your needs for customization, you can provide custom components. For this, the editor provides the following slots:

*   `background` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/editor/Background.vue)
    
*   `toolbar` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/toolbar/Toolbar.vue)
    
*   `palette` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/nodepalette/NodePalette.vue)
    
*   `connection` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/connection/ConnectionWrapper.vue)
    *   Props:
        *   `connection` (type: `[Connection](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Connection.html) `)
*   `temporaryConnection` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/connection/TemporaryConnection.vue)
    *   Props:
        *   `temporaryConnection` (type: `[ITemporaryConnection](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.ITemporaryConnection.html)  | null`)
*   `node` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/node/Node.vue)
    *   Props:
        *   `node` (type: `[AbstractNode](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.AbstractNode.html) `)
        *   `selected` (type: `boolean`)
        *   `select` (type: `() => void`) callback for node being selected
*   `sidebar` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/sidebar/Sidebar.vue)
    
*   `minimap` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/components/Minimap.vue)
    
*   `contextMenu` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/components/ContextMenu.vue)
    *   Props:
        *   `contextMenu` (type: return value of [`useContextMenu`](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/contextMenu.ts)
            )

There are other components that provide slots as well:

*   Node
    *   `nodeInterface` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/node/NodeInterface.vue)
        *   Props:
            *   `type` (type: `"input"|"output"`)
            *   `node` (type: `[AbstractNode](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.AbstractNode.html) `)
            *   `intf` (type: `[NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html) `)
*   NodeInterface
    *   `portTooltip` [(default component)](https://github.com/newcat/baklavajs/blob/master/packages/renderer-vue/src/node/NodeInterface.vue#L11-L13)
        *   Props:
            *   `showTooltip` (type: `boolean`)

So, for example, if you want to use a custom component for a certain node type, you could do it like this:

vue

    <template>
        <BaklavaEditor>
            <template #node="nodeProps">
                <MyNodeRenderer v-if="nodeProps.node.type === 'MyNodeType'" :key="nodeProps.node.id" v-bind="nodeProps" />
                <BaklavaNode v-else :key="nodeProps.node.id" v-bind="nodeProps" />
            </template>
        </BaklavaEditor>
    </template>
    
    <script setup>
    import { BaklavaEditor, Components } from "@baklavajs/renderer-vue";
    const BaklavaNode = Components.Node;
    
    // example, replace with your component:
    import MyNodeRenderer from "./MyNodeRenderer.vue";
    </script>

List of CSS Classes [​](https://baklava.tech/visual-editor/customization.html#list-of-css-classes)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Below you can find a list of CSS classes used in Baklava:

*   **Editor:**
    *   `baklava-editor`: Base class for the editor
*   **Nodes:**
    *   `baklava-node`: Base class for each node
    *   `--selected`: Applied when a node is selected
    *   `--dragging`: Applied when a node is being dragged
    *   `--two-column`: Applied if a node is a two-column node
    *   `--palette`: Applied to a node if it is used as an entry in the node palette
    *   `__title`: Title (top-bar) of a node
        *   `__title-label`: Actual title (label) of the node
        *   `__menu`: Contains the three dots (menu button) on the right side of each node
    *   `__content`: Container for the inputs and outputs of the node
        *   `__inputs`: Container for all inputs
        *   `__outputs`: Container for all outputs
*   **Node Interfaces:**
    *   `baklava-node-interface`: Base class for each node interface
    *   `--input`: Applied when the node interface is an input
    *   `--output`: Applied when the node interface is an output
    *   `--connected`: Applied when the node interface has a connection
    *   `__port`: The "dot" via which the node interface can be connected
    *   `__tooltip`: The tooltip that is shown when hovering over the node interface
*   **Connection:**
    *   `baklava-connection`: Base class for each connection
    *   `--temporary`: Applied when the connection is still being dragged (in the process of being created or changed)
    *   `--allowed`: Applied when the connection can be created (the default styles display the connection green in this case)
    *   `--forbidden`: Applied when the connection can not be created (the default styles display the connection red in this case) or when this connection would be destroyed when creating a different connection
*   **Sidebar:**
    *   `baklava-sidebar`: Base class for the sidebar
    *   `--open`: Applied when the sidebar should be visible
    *   `__resizer`: Handle for resizing the sidebar
    *   `__header`: Header of the sidebar.
        *   `__close`: Close button
        *   `__node-name`: The title of the currently selected node
    *   `__interface`: Each interface shown in the sidebar
*   **Toolbar:**
    *   `baklava-toolbar`: Base class for the toolbar
    *   `baklava-toolbar-entry`: Base class for each entry in the toolbar
    *   `baklava-toolbar-button`: This class is applied to every entry that is clickable
*   **Others:**
    *   `baklava-node-palette`: Base class for the node palette

---

### `Protected`addInput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.AbstractNode.html#addinput)

    ): boolean[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.AbstractNode.html#addinput-1)
    
    Add an input interface to the node
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   key: string
        
        Key of the input
        
    *   input: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)

    #### Returns boolean
    
    True when the input was added, otherwise false (prevented by an event handler)

Enumeration Members
-------------------

### Idle[](https://baklava.tech/api/enums/_baklavajs_engine.EngineStatus.html#idle)

Idle: "Idle"

The engine is not currently running a calculation but will do so when the graph changes

### Paused[](https://baklava.tech/api/enums/_baklavajs_engine.EngineStatus.html#paused)

Paused: "Paused"

The engine is temporarily paused

### Running[](https://baklava.tech/api/enums/_baklavajs_engine.EngineStatus.html#running)

Running: "Running"

The engine is currently running a calculation

### Stopped[](https://baklava.tech/api/enums/_baklavajs_engine.EngineStatus.html#stopped)

Stopped: "Stopped"

The engine is not running

    \>,  
    \>
    
    This event is called after a node has been calculated.
    
*   ##### afterRun: BaklavaEvent<CalculationResult, [BaseEngine](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html)
    <[CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)
    , [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
    \>\>
    
    This event is called as soon as a run is completed. The argument is the result of the calculation.
    
*   ##### beforeNodeCalculation: BaklavaEvent<  
        [BeforeNodeCalculationEventData](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_engine.BeforeNodeCalculationEventData.html)

    , [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
    \>,  
    \>
    
    This event is called before a node is calculated. It is not preventable since this would break calculation.
    
*   ##### beforeRun: PreventableBaklavaEvent<  
        [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)

    , [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
    \>,  
    \>
    
    This event will be called before all the nodes `calculate` functions are called. The argument is the calculationData that the nodes will receive

Methods

### calculateOrder[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#calculateorder)

*   calculateOrder(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#calculateorder-1)
    
    Force the engine to recalculate the node execution order before the next run. This is normally done automatically. Use this method if the default change detection does not work in your scenario.
    
    #### Returns void
    

### `Protected`calculateWithoutData[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#calculatewithoutdata)

*   calculateWithoutData(  
        ...args: [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
    ,  
    ): Promise<CalculationResult | null\>[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#calculatewithoutdata-1)
    
    Use the `gatherCalculationData` hook to get the calculation data
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   ...args: [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
        
        The calculation arguments with which the engine's calculate method will be called (in addition to the `calculationData`)
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<CalculationResult | null\>
    
    The calculation result
    

### checkConnection[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#checkconnection)

*   checkConnection(  
        from: NodeInterface,  
        to: NodeInterface,  
    ): CheckConnectionHookResult[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#checkconnection-1)
    
    Check whether a connection can be created. A connection can not be created when it would result in a cyclic graph.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   from: NodeInterface
        
        The interface from which the connection would start
        
    *   to: NodeInterface
        
        The interface where the connection would end
        
    
    #### Returns CheckConnectionHookResult
    
    Whether the connection can be created
    

### `Protected` `Abstract`execute[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#execute)

*   execute(  
        calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)
    ,  
        ...calculationArgs: [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
    ,  
    ): Promise<CalculationResult\>[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#execute-1)
    
    Overwrite this method to perform the calculation
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)
        
        The data which is provided to each node's `calculate` method
        
    *   ...calculationArgs: [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
        
        Additional data which is only provided to the engine
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<CalculationResult\>
    
    The calculation result
    

### `Abstract`getInputValues[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#getinputvalues)

*   getInputValues(graph: Graph): Map<string, any\>[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#getinputvalues-1)
    
    Gathers the values of all unconnected input interfaces in the graph
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   graph: Graph
    
    #### Returns Map<string, any\>
    
    Map [nodeInterface.id](http://nodeinterface.id/)
     -> value
    

### `Protected` `Abstract`onChange[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#onchange)

*   onChange(  
        recalculateOrder: boolean,  
        updatedNode?: AbstractNode,  
        data?: INodeUpdateEventData,  
    ): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#onchange-1)
    
    This method is called whenever the graph or values of node interfaces have been changed. You can overwrite this method to automatically trigger a calculation on change. Note: This method is only called when the engine is either idle or running.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   recalculateOrder: boolean
        
        Whether the change modified the graph itself, e. g. a connection or a node was added/removed
        
    *   `Optional`updatedNode: AbstractNode
        
        If a node was updated (which means the value a node's interface has been changed): the node that was updated; `undefined` otherwise
        
    *   `Optional`data: INodeUpdateEventData
        
        If a node was updated: The `update` event payload to determine, which interface exactly has been changed; `undefined` otherwise
        
    
    #### Returns void
    

### pause[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#pause)

*   pause(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#pause-1)
    
    Temporarily pause the engine. Use this method when you want to update the graph with the calculation results.
    
    #### Returns void
    

### resume[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#resume)

*   resume(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#resume-1)
    
    Resume the engine from the paused state
    
    #### Returns void
    

### `Abstract`runGraph[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#rungraph)

*   runGraph(  
        graph: Graph,  
        inputs: Map<string, any\>,  
        calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)
    ,  
    ): Promise<CalculationResult\>[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#rungraph-1)
    
    Run a non-root graph. This method can be used by nodes to calculate internal graphs (e. g. GraphNode). DO NOT use this method for calculation of the root graph! It won't emit any events.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   graph: Graph
        
        The graph to execute
        
    *   inputs: Map<string, any\>
        
        Map<NodeInterfaceId, value>
        
    *   calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)
        
        The data which is provided to each node's `calculate` method
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<CalculationResult\>
    
    A promise that resolves to a map that maps rootNodes to their calculated value (what the calculation function of the node returned)
    

### runOnce[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#runonce)

*   runOnce(  
        calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)
    ,  
        ...args: [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
    ,  
    ): Promise<CalculationResult | null\>[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#runonce-1)
    
    Calculate all nodes once. This will automatically calculate the node calculation order if necessary and transfer values between connected node interfaces.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationdata)
        
        The data which is provided to each node's `calculate` method
        
    *   ...args: [CalculationArgs](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#constructorbaseenginecalculationargs)
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<CalculationResult | null\>
    
    A promise that resolves to either
    
    *   a map from each node's id to its calculated value (what the calculation function of the node returned)
    *   null if the calculation was prevented from the beforeRun event
    

### start[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#start)

*   start(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#start-1)
    
    Start the engine. After started, it will run everytime the graph is changed.
    
    #### Returns void
    

### stop[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#stop)

*   stop(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#stop-1)
    
    Stop the engine
    
    #### Returns void
    

### `Protected`validateNodeCalculationOutput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#validatenodecalculationoutput)

*   validateNodeCalculationOutput(node: AbstractNode, output: any): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.BaseEngine.html#validatenodecalculationoutput-1)
    
    Validate the result of a node's `calculate` method. A result is valid if:
    
    *   is has the correct format (it must be an object, where the key is the interface key and the value is the output value for that interface)
    *   every output interface has a value assigned to it (null and undefined are also valid, but the key must exist in the object)
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   node: AbstractNode
        
        The node which produced the output data
        
    *   output: any
        
        The result of the node's `calculate` method
        
    
    #### Returns void

*   Inherited

#### Type Declaration

    <[CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#constructordependencyenginecalculationdata)
    , \[\]\>\>
    
    This event is called as soon as a run is completed. The argument is the result of the calculation.
    
*   ##### beforeNodeCalculation: BaklavaEvent<[BeforeNodeCalculationEventData](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_engine.BeforeNodeCalculationEventData.html)

    , \[\]\>\>
    
    This event is called before a node is calculated. It is not preventable since this would break calculation.

    <[CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#constructordependencyenginecalculationdata)
    , \[\]\>\>

### calculateOrder[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#calculateorder)

*   calculateOrder(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#calculateorder-1)
    
    Force the engine to recalculate the node execution order before the next run. This is normally done automatically. Use this method if the default change detection does not work in your scenario.
    
    #### Returns void

        from: NodeInterface,  
        to: NodeInterface,  
    ): CheckConnectionHookResult[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#checkconnection-1)

        The interface from which the connection would start
        
    *   to: NodeInterface

### `Protected`onChange[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#onchange)

*   onChange(recalculateOrder: boolean): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#onchange-1)
    
    This method is called whenever the graph or values of node interfaces have been changed. You can overwrite this method to automatically trigger a calculation on change. Note: This method is only called when the engine is either idle or running.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   recalculateOrder: boolean
        
        Whether the change modified the graph itself, e. g. a connection or a node was added/removed
        
    
    #### Returns void
    

### pause[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#pause)

*   pause(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#pause-1)
    
    Temporarily pause the engine. Use this method when you want to update the graph with the calculation results.
    
    #### Returns void

### runGraph[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#rungraph)

*   runGraph(  
        graph: Graph,  
        inputs: Map<string, any\>,  
        calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#constructordependencyenginecalculationdata)
    ,  
    ): Promise<CalculationResult\>[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#rungraph-1)
    
    Run a non-root graph. This method can be used by nodes to calculate internal graphs (e. g. GraphNode). DO NOT use this method for calculation of the root graph! It won't emit any events.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   graph: Graph
        
        The graph to execute
        
    *   inputs: Map<string, any\>
        
        Map<NodeInterfaceId, value>
        
    *   calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#constructordependencyenginecalculationdata)
        
        The data which is provided to each node's `calculate` method
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<CalculationResult\>
    
    A promise that resolves to a map that maps rootNodes to their calculated value (what the calculation function of the node returned)
    

### runOnce[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#runonce)

*   runOnce(  
        calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#constructordependencyenginecalculationdata)
    ,  
        ...args: \[\],  
    ): Promise<CalculationResult | null\>[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#runonce-1)
    
    Calculate all nodes once. This will automatically calculate the node calculation order if necessary and transfer values between connected node interfaces.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   calculationData: [CalculationData](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#constructordependencyenginecalculationdata)
        
        The data which is provided to each node's `calculate` method
        
    *   ...args: \[\]
    
    #### Returns Promise<CalculationResult | null\>
    
    A promise that resolves to either
    
    *   a map from each node's id to its calculated value (what the calculation function of the node returned)
    *   null if the calculation was prevented from the beforeRun event
    

### start[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#start)

*   start(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#start-1)
    
    Start the engine. After started, it will run everytime the graph is changed.
    
    #### Returns void
    

### stop[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#stop)

*   stop(): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#stop-1)
    
    Stop the engine
    
    #### Returns void
    

### `Protected`validateNodeCalculationOutput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#validatenodecalculationoutput)

*   validateNodeCalculationOutput(node: AbstractNode, output: any): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_engine.DependencyEngine.html#validatenodecalculationoutput-1)
    
    Validate the result of a node's `calculate` method. A result is valid if:
    
    *   is has the correct format (it must be an object, where the key is the interface key and the value is the output value for that interface)
    *   every output interface has a value assigned to it (null and undefined are also valid, but the key must exist in the object)
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   node: AbstractNode
        
        The node which produced the output data
        
    *   output: any
        
        The result of the node's `calculate` method
        
    
    #### Returns void
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited

ThemeOSLightDark

    ): boolean[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.DynamicNode.html#addinput-1)
    
    Add an input interface to the node
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   key: string
        
        Key of the input
        
    *   input: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)

    #### Returns boolean
    
    True when the input was added, otherwise false (prevented by an event handler)

### `Optional`calculate[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.GraphInputNode.html#calculate)

calculate?: [CalculateFunction](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_core.CalculateFunction.html)
<  
    { name: string },  
    { placeholder: any },  
    [CalculationContext](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.CalculationContext.html)
<any, [IEngine](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IEngine.html)
<any\>\>,  
\>

The default implementation does nothing. Overwrite this method to do calculation.

#### Param: inputs[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.GraphInputNode.html#param-inputs)

Values of all input interfaces

#### Param: globalValues[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.GraphInputNode.html#param-globalvalues)

### `Protected`addInput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.GraphInputNode.html#addinput)

*   addInput(key: string, input: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
    ): boolean[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.GraphInputNode.html#addinput-1)
    
    Add an input interface to the node
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   key: string
        
        Key of the input
        
    *   input: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
        
        The input instance
        
    
    #### Returns boolean
    
    True when the input was added, otherwise false (prevented by an event handler)

### `Optional`calculate[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#calculate)

calculate?: [CalculateFunction](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_core.CalculateFunction.html)
<Dynamic<[I](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#i)
\>, Dynamic<[O](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#o)
\>\>

This function is called by the engine with the input values. It should perform the necessary calculation and then return the output values

### onUpdate[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#onupdate)

onUpdate: (  
    this: [DynamicNode](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.DynamicNode.html)
<[I](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#i)
, [O](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#o)
\>,  
    inputs: [I](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#i)
,  
    outputs: [O](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IDynamicNodeDefinition.html#o)
,  
) \=> [DynamicNodeUpdateResult](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.DynamicNodeUpdateResult.html)

This function is called whenever the value of one of the static input or output interfaces is changed. It should return a definition for every dynamic interface based on the values of the static interfaces.

### `Optional`calculate[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#calculate)

calculate?: [CalculateFunction](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_core.CalculateFunction.html)
<[I](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#constructornodei)
, [O](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#constructornodeo)
, [CalculationContext](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.CalculationContext.html)
<any, [IEngine](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IEngine.html)
<any\>\>\>

The default implementation does nothing. Overwrite this method to do calculation.

#### Param: inputs[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#param-inputs)

Values of all input interfaces

#### Param: globalValues[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#param-globalvalues)

Set of values passed to every node by the engine plugin

#### Returns[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#returns)

Values for output interfaces

     | undefined
    
    The graph instance the node is placed in. `undefined` if the node hasn't been placed in a graph yet.

### `Protected`addInput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#addinput)

*   addInput(key: string, input: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
    ): boolean[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#addinput-1)
    
    Add an input interface to the node
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   key: string
        
        Key of the input
        
    *   input: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
        
        The input instance
        
    
    #### Returns boolean
    
    True when the input was added, otherwise false (prevented by an event handler)
    

### `Protected`addOutput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#addoutput)

*   addOutput(key: string, output: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
    ): boolean[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Node.html#addoutput-1)
    
    Add an output interface to the node
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   key: string
        
        Key of the output
        
    *   output: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
        
        The output instance
        
    
    #### Returns boolean
    
    True when the output was added, otherwise false (prevented by an event handler)

        options?: [IRegisterNodeTypeOptions](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IRegisterNodeTypeOptions.html)
    ,  
    ): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Editor.html#registernodetype-1)
    
    Register a new node type
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   type: [AbstractNodeConstructor](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_core.AbstractNodeConstructor.html)
        
        Actual type / constructor of the node
        
    *   `Optional`options: [IRegisterNodeTypeOptions](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_core.IRegisterNodeTypeOptions.html)
        
        Optionally specify a title and/or a category for this node
        
    
    #### Returns void

### checkConnection[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.Graph.html#checkconnection)

    #### Parameters
    
    *   from: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)

    *   to: [NodeInterface](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_core.NodeInterface.html)
        <any\>

        \>\>

    #### Parameters

    *   callback: [EventListener](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_events.EventListener.html)

===================================

### emit[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_events.PreventableBaklavaEvent.html#emit)

*   emit(data: [T](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_events.PreventableBaklavaEvent.html#constructorpreventablebaklavaeventt)
    ): { prevented: boolean }[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_events.PreventableBaklavaEvent.html#emit-1)
    
    Invoke all listeners.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   data: [T](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_events.PreventableBaklavaEvent.html#constructorpreventablebaklavaeventt)
        
        The data to invoke all listeners with
        
    
    #### Returns { prevented: boolean }
    
    An object, where the `prevented` field is `true` when one of the listeners requested to prevent the event, otherwise `false`

# SequentialHook | Reference - BaklavaJS

*   [@baklavajs/events](https://baklava.tech/api/modules/_baklavajs_events.html)
    
*   [SequentialHook](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_events.SequentialHook.html)
    

Class SequentialHook<I, E, O>
=============================

This class will run the taps one after each other and pass the data from every subscriber to another.

#### Type Parameters

*   I
*   E
*   O extends [I](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_events.SequentialHook.html#constructorsequentialhooki)

        Type to convert to
        
    *   transformationFunction: (value: [T](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_interface-types.NodeInterfaceType.html#constructornodeinterfacetypet)
        ) \=> [O](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_interface-types.NodeInterfaceType.html#addconversiono)
         = ...
        
        Will be called to transform the value from one type to another. A transformation to convert the type `string` to `number` could be `parseInt`.
        
    
    #### Returns [NodeInterfaceType](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_interface-types.NodeInterfaceType.html)
    <[T](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_interface-types.NodeInterfaceType.html#constructornodeinterfacetypet)
    \>
    
    the instance the method was called on for chaining
    

### Settings

*   Inherited

### `Protected`addInput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.SubgraphOutputNode.html#addinput)

*   addInput(key: string, input: NodeInterface): boolean[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.SubgraphOutputNode.html#addinput-1)

        Key of the input
        
    *   input: NodeInterface

### `Protected`addOutput[](https://baklava.tech/api/classes/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.SubgraphOutputNode.html#addoutput)

    *   output: NodeInterface
        
        The output instance
        
    
    #### Returns boolean
    
    True when the output was added, otherwise false (prevented by an event handler)

### registerHotkey[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ICommandHandler.html#registerhotkey)

*   registerHotkey(  
        keys: string\[\],  
        commandName: string,  
        options?: HotkeyRegistrationOptions,  
    ): void[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ICommandHandler.html#registerhotkey-1)
    
    Register a new hotkey combination for the command.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   keys: string\[\]
        
        Combination of keys. When all keys in the given array are pressed at the same time, the command will be executed.
        
    *   commandName: string
        
        Name of the command that should be executed when the keys are pressed.
        
    *   `Optional`options: HotkeyRegistrationOptions
        
        Options for the hotkey registration.
        
    
    #### Returns void

# IViewSettings | Reference - BaklavaJS

*   [@baklavajs/renderer-vue](https://baklava.tech/api/modules/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.html)
    
*   [IViewSettings](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html)
    

Interface IViewSettings
=======================

interface IViewSettings {  
    [background](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#background)
: {  
        gridDivision: number;  
        gridSize: number;  
        subGridVisibleThreshold: number;  
    };  
    [contextMenu](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#contextmenu)
: { additionalItems: [ContextMenuItem](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ContextMenuItem.html)
\[\]; enabled: boolean };  
    [displayValueOnHover](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#displayvalueonhover)
: boolean;  
    [enableMinimap](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#enableminimap)
: boolean;  
    [nodes](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#nodes)
: {  
        defaultWidth: number;  
        maxWidth: number;  
        minWidth: number;  
        resizable: boolean;  
        reverseY: boolean;  
    };  
    [palette](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#palette)
: { enabled: boolean };  
    [panZoom](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#panzoom)
: { maxScale: number; minScale: number };  
    [sidebar](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#sidebar)
: { enabled: boolean; resizable: boolean; width: number };  
    [toolbar](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#toolbar)
: {  
        commands: [ToolbarCommand](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ToolbarCommand.html)
\[\];  
        enabled: boolean;  
        subgraphCommands: [ToolbarCommand](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ToolbarCommand.html)
\[\];  
    };  
    [useStraightConnections](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#usestraightconnections)
: boolean;  
    [zoomToFit](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#zoomtofit)
: {  
        paddingBottom: number;  
        paddingLeft: number;  
        paddingRight: number;  
        paddingTop: number;  
    };  
}

background: {

Background settings

### contextMenu[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#contextmenu)

contextMenu: { additionalItems: [ContextMenuItem](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ContextMenuItem.html)
\[\]; enabled: boolean }

#### Type Declaration

*   ##### additionalItems: [ContextMenuItem](https://baklava.tech/api/types/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ContextMenuItem.html)
    \[\]
    
*   ##### enabled: boolean
    
    Whether the context menu should be enabled
    

### displayValueOnHover[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#displayvalueonhover)

displayValueOnHover: boolean

Show interface value on port hover

### enableMinimap[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#enableminimap)

enableMinimap: boolean

Show a minimap

### nodes[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#nodes)

nodes: {  
    defaultWidth: number;  
    maxWidth: number;  
    minWidth: number;  
    resizable: boolean;  
    reverseY: boolean;  
}

Node settings

#### Type Declaration

*   ##### defaultWidth: number
    
    Default width of a node
    
*   ##### maxWidth: number
    
    Maximum width of a node
    
*   ##### minWidth: number
    
    Minimum width of a node
    
*   ##### resizable: boolean
    
    Whether users should be able to resize nodes
    
*   ##### reverseY: boolean
    
    Inverts the order of inputs/outputs in nodes.
    

### palette[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#palette)

palette: { enabled: boolean }

Palette settings

#### Type Declaration

*   ##### enabled: boolean
    
    Whether the palette should be enabled
    

### panZoom[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#panzoom)

panZoom: { maxScale: number; minScale: number }

sidebar: { enabled: boolean; resizable: boolean; width: number }

Sidebar settings

#### Type Declaration

*   ##### enabled: boolean
    
    Whether the sidebar should be enabled
    
*   ##### resizable: boolean
    
    Whether users should be able to resize the sidebar
    
*   ##### width: number
    
    Width of the sidebar in pixels
    

### toolbar[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#toolbar)

toolbar: {  
    commands: [ToolbarCommand](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ToolbarCommand.html)

    enabled: boolean;  
    subgraphCommands: [ToolbarCommand](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.ToolbarCommand.html)
\[\];  
}

Toolbar settings

    \[\]
    
*   ##### enabled: boolean

### useStraightConnections[](https://baklava.tech/api/interfaces/_baklavajs_renderer-vue.IViewSettings.html#usestraightconnections)

useStraightConnections: boolean
